NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

GERMANISCHER LLOYD INDUSTRIAL SERVICES INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED.

Registered Office: Old No. 304-305, New No. 443, Anna Salai, Teynampet, Chennai-600 018.
Pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, notice is hereby given that at an Extra-ordinary General Meeting
of the Company held on 5th March 2016, the following Special Resolution was passed unanimously to voluntarily wind up
GERMANISCHER LLOYD INDUSTRIAL SERVICES INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 4th February 2016, made by the Board of
Directors of the Company under section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956 and section 305 of the Companies Act, 2013,
stating that the Company would be able to pay debts in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof,
the Company, having its Registered Office at Old No. 304-305, New No. 443, Anna Salai, Guna Building, Teynampet,
Chennai-600 018, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484 (1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and Section 304(b)
of the Companies Act, 2013.
Chennai,
11th March 2016.

R. RAMESH KUMAR,
Director.
